CREATE TABLE `beast` (
  `B_ID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `B_NEV` text COLLATE latin2_hungarian_ci NOT NULL,
  `B_STR` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_AGI` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_DEX` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_DEF` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_REF` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_CON` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_INT` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_LUC` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_MANA` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_DB` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_HP` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_XP` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `B_ELEM` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',

  `B_LVL` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1'
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin2 COLLATE=latin2_hungarian_ci;
